    "3": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">3</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Tu in Tiberius Caesar a maan zawh kum sawm le kum nga a cin kumin Pontius Pilate in Judea gam mangpipa ahi hi. Herod in Galilee gam uk mangpa hi a, a naupa Philip in Iturea gam le Trachonitis gam uk mangpa hi in, Lysanias in Abilene gam uk mangpa ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Annas le Caiaphas in Siampi Ukte ahih laitak un gamlak a om Zacharias tapa John tungah Pasian thu a tung hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Jordan gun kuam mun khempeuh ah John vak kawikawi a, mawhmai nadingin kisikkikna tawh kisai tui kiphumna thu a hilh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Hih in kamsangpa Isaiah laibu sunga kigelhsa thu ahi hi. Tualai ah, “Gamlak a kikopa awging in, ‘Topa pai nading lam na sial unla, A lampite na tangsak un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Muallian mualneu khempeuh kitamsak in, Mualkuam khempeuh kivuk dim ding hi. A komna munte kivukdim in, Lamkawite kitangsak dinga,</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Mi khempeuh in Pasian hotkhiatna a mu ding uh hi,’ ” ci in a kigelh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">Tua ciangin John in tui kiphumsak dingin ama kianga hong pai mihonpite kiangah, “A gupha gul suante aw! A hong tung ding hehna pan a taikhia dingin kua in hong hilhkhol ahi hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"8\"><sup data-verseid=\"8\">&nbsp;<!-- -->8<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"8\">Tua ahih manin kisikkikna tawh a kituak gah na gah un. Note lungsim sungah, ‘Abraham ka pa uh hi,’ ci in suang kei un. Ken kong cih in ah Pasian in hih suangte nangawn Abraham tate a suaksak thei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"9\"><sup data-verseid=\"9\">&nbsp;<!-- -->9<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"9\">Tu mahmah in zong singphung tengah hei kinga zo hi. Kua na hi hiam cih kong thei uha Pasian mi Siangthopa na hi hi,” ci in nakpi in a kiko hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"35\"><sup data-verseid=\"35\">&nbsp;<!-- -->35<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"35\">Ahih hangin Zeisu in, “Pau kei inla, ama sung pan paikhia in,” ci in a taii hi. Tua dawi in mite laizang ah tua pa sawnpai a, liamsak loin a paikhia hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"36\"><sup data-verseid=\"36\">&nbsp;<!-- -->36<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"36\">Tua ciangin amaute khempeuh in lamdangsa mahmah uh a, “Hih kammal in bangci bang ahi hiam? Thuneihna le vangliatna tawh dawigilote thu a piak ciangin a paikhia hi,” a kici uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"37\"><sup data-verseid=\"37\">&nbsp;<!-- -->37<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"37\">Ama thu tua kima om gam khempeuh ah a thang hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"38\"><sup data-verseid=\"38\">&nbsp;<!-- -->38<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"38\">Tu in kikhopna inn panin Zeisu paikhia a, Simon inn ah a lut hi. Simon sunghnu nattun in a cisa a, gim mahmah ahih manin a damsak nadingin a ngen uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"39\"><sup data-verseid=\"39\">&nbsp;<!-- -->39<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"39\">Tua nu gei ah Zeisu dingin cisa natna a taii ciangin a natna a dam hi. Tua ciangin amah thokhia pahin amaute zin a do hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"40\"><sup data-verseid=\"40\">&nbsp;<!-- -->40<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"40\">Nitum khit ciangin natna tuamtuam a vei cina khempeuh ama kiangah hong puak uh a, amaute khatciat tungah a khut nga in a damsak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"41\"><sup data-verseid=\"41\">&nbsp;<!-- -->41<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"41\">Dawite in zong, “Pasian Tapa Khazih na hi hi!” ci in kiko in mi tampi sung pan a paikhia uh hi. Dawite in Khazih ahihlam thei uh ahih manin amah in amaute taii in kam khat beek a pausak kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"42\"><sup data-verseid=\"42\">&nbsp;<!-- -->42<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"42\">Khua a vak ciangin amah tua mun panin gamdaihna mun khatah a pai hi. Mihonpite in amah zong uha a kiang a tun uh ciangin amaute a paisan loh nadingin a kho uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"43\"><sup data-verseid=\"43\">&nbsp;<!-- -->43<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"43\">Ahih hangin amah in amaute kiangah, “Pasian kumpigam thu khuadangte ah zong ka tangko loh phamawh hi. Banghang hiam cihleh tua na a sem dingin a hong kisawl ahi hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"44\"><sup data-verseid=\"44\">&nbsp;<!-- -->44<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"44\">Tua bangin Galilee gam sunga kikhopna innteng ah thu a hilh kawikawi hi.</span></span></div><section class=\"information\"><button class=\"information-toggle\" type=\"button\">Copyrighted Material<!-- -->&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class=\"learn-more\">Learn More</span><svg class=\"icon\"><use xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" xlink:href=\"/svglist.svg#arrow_down\"></use></svg></button><div aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"rah-static rah-static--height-zero \" style=\"height:0;overflow:hidden\"><div><div style=\"max-height:0\" class=\"copyrights-section\"><div class=\"ot-copyright\"></div><div class=\"nt-copyright\"></div></div></div></div><div class=\"ministry-statement\"><div class=\"ministry-tagline\">©<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"http://www.bible.is\">Bible.is</a>, a ministry of<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.faithcomesbyhearing.com\">Faith Comes By Hearing</a>&nbsp;<!-- -->®.<!-- -->&nbsp;</div><div class=\"ministry-terms-support\"><a id=\"terms-of-service\" href=\"/terms\">Terms and Conditions</a>&nbsp; | &nbsp;<a href=\"https://support.bible.is/contact\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" id=\"help-support\">Help &amp; Support</a></div></div></section></main>",
    "5": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">5</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Gennesaret tuili gei ah Zeisu a din laitak in Pasian thu ngai dinga hong kikhawm mihonpi in amah a nehcip gawp uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Amah in ngabengte ngen sawp dinga a paikal un tuili gei‑a om gunkuang nih a mu hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Tua gunkuang nihte lak panin Simon gunkuang ah amah kah in lei tawh tawmkha gunkuang a kihalsak nadingin a ngen hi. Tua khit ciangin gunkuang tungah tu in mihonpite thu a hilh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Thu a gen khit ciangin Simon kiangah, “Tui thukna lamah gunkuang khin inla na ngen khuh in,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Ahih hangin Simon in, “Sia aw, zan thapai hanciamtak in ka khuh uh hangin khat beek ka man kei uh hi. Ahi zongin na cih bangin ka khuh ding hi,” ci in a dawng hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Tua bangin ngen a khuh uh leh ngasa tampi khuh kha uh a, a ngen uh a kikek hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">Tua ciangin gunkuang dang khat a om a lawmte hong pai in a huh nading uh khutvan in sam uh a, a lawmte zong hong pai uh hi. Gunkuang nih a dim tuakin ngasa guang uh ahih manin gunkuangte a tum dektak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"8\"><sup data-verseid=\"8\">&nbsp;<!-- -->8<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"8\">Simon Peter in hih thupiang a muh ciangin Zeisu khephung ah kunsuk a, “Topa aw, mawhnei mi ka hih manin ka kiang panin kihemkhia in!” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"9\"><sup data-verseid=\"9\">&nbsp;<!-- -->9<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"9\">Banghang hiam cihleh amah le a lawmte khempeuh in a ngasa mat uh lamdang a sa mahmah uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"10\"><sup data-verseid=\"10\">&nbsp;<!-- -->10<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"10\">Simon lawmte ahi Zebedee tate James le John in zong lamdang a sa mahmah uh hi. Tua ciangin Zeisu in Simon kiangah, “Lau kei in. Tu a kipan in mite na man ta ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">A gunkuangte uh tuigei a tut khit uh ciangin na khempeuh nusia in ama nung a zui uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Khua khatah Zeisu a om laitak in a pumtang a phak mi khatin amah a muh ciangin boksuk a, “Topa aw, hong damsak nuam lecin nong damsak thei hi,” ci in nakpitak in a thum hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">Tua ciangin, Zeisu in a khut zanin amah lawng a, “Kong damsak nuam hi, damta in,” ci in thu a pia hi. Tua ciangin tua pa phaknatna a dam pah hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Tua ciangin Zeisu in tua thu kuama kiangah a gen loh nadingin thupia a, “Siampipa kiangah va kilak inla, na damna hangin Moses thupiak bangin biakpiakna va nei in. Tua in amau aa dingin teci ahi ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">Ahih hangin, ama thu kizel semsem a, a thugen ngai ding le a natnate uh ama damsak ding ut in mihonpi a hong kikhawm uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"16\"><sup data-verseid=\"16\">&nbsp;<!-- -->16<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"16\">Amah ahih leh gamlak ah paikhia in thu a ngen zelzel hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"17\"><sup data-verseid=\"17\">&nbsp;<!-- -->17<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"17\">Ni khat Zeisu thuhilh a a om laitak in Jerusalem khuapi a kipan Galilee gam le Judea gam khempeuh panin a hong kisutuah Pharisee pawlte le thukhamhilh siate ama kiangah a tu uh hi. Amaute lau mahmah uh a, “Tuni‑a i muh nate lamdang thei mahmah hi,” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"27\"><sup data-verseid=\"27\">&nbsp;<!-- -->27<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"27\">Hih thuteng khit ciangin Zeisu paikhia a, siahdonna buukah tu a om Levi kici siahdongpa khat a muh ciangin tuapa kiangah, “Hong zui in,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"28\"><sup data-verseid=\"28\">&nbsp;<!-- -->28<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"28\">Amah dingkhia a, a na khempeuh nusia in Zeisu a zui hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"29\"><sup data-verseid=\"29\">&nbsp;<!-- -->29<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"29\">Tua ciangin Levi in a inn ah Zeisu annekpihna thupitak in a bawl hi. Puan thak le puan lui a kituak thei kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"37\"><sup data-verseid=\"37\">&nbsp;<!-- -->37<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"37\">Kuamah in savun um lui sungah lenggahtui thak a thun kei hi.     "6": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">6</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Sabbath masa pen khit a nihna Sabbath ni in buhlei khat kantan a Zeisu a pai laitak in a nungzuite in buhvuite zut uha a khut sungah nuai in a bak uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Pharisee pawlte pawlkhat in amaute kiangah, “Sabbath ni in sep dinga thukham in a phalloh nasep banghang in sem na hi uh hiam?” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Tua ciangin Zeisu in, “David in a pawlte tawh a gilkial laitak un,</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Pasian inn sungah lutin siampite longal midang in a nek theih ding a hilo Ompihna Anlumte la in ne a, a pawlte zong pia hi cih thu sim ngeilo na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Tua khit ciangin Zeisu in amaute kiangah, “Mihing Tapa in Sabbath a Ukpa zong ahi hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">A dang Sabbath ni khat in kikhopna inn sungah Zeisu lutin thu a hilh hi. Tualai ah a taklam khut a keugaw pasal khat a om hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">Thukhamhilh siate le Pharisee pawlte in Sabbath ni peuhmah a Zeisu in cina a damsak leh a mawhmat dingin a encik gige uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"8\"><sup data-verseid=\"8\">&nbsp;<!-- -->8<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"8\">Ahih hangin Zeisu in amaute ngaihsutna thei ahih manin a khut a sipa kiangah, “Tho inla, a laizang ah hong ding in,” a cih ciangin amah tho in a ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"9\"><sup data-verseid=\"9\">&nbsp;<!-- -->9<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"9\">Tua khit ciangin Zeisu in amaute kiangah, “Thu khat kong dong ding hi Sabbath ni in a pha bawl ding le a sia bawl ding, nuntakna gup ding le thah ding koi pen thukham tawh kituak zaw ahi hiam?” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"10\"><sup data-verseid=\"10\">&nbsp;<!-- -->10<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"10\">Amah in amaute khempeuh a gualet khit ciangin tua pa kiangah, “Na khut zankhia in,” a ci hi. Tua pa in a khut a zan leh a lang khat lam mah bangin dam a, a ngeina a bangkik hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">Ahih hangin amaute hehlua uh ahih manin, “Zeisu bang cih ding i hi hiam?” ci in a kikum uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span Misite thokik in mizawngte tungah lungdamna thu kitangko hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"23\"><sup data-verseid=\"23\">&nbsp;<!-- -->23<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"23\">Keima hanga a puklo mi in mihampha ahi hi,” ci in a dawng hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"24\"><sup data-verseid=\"24\">&nbsp;<!-- -->24<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"24\">John kamtaite a ciah khit uh ciangin, Zeisu in mihonpite kiangah John thu a gen in ah, “Gamlak ah bang en dinga pai na hi uh hiam? Huih in a mut cianga a kihuang diamdiam pumpeng kung peuh a en dinga pai na hi uh hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"25\"><sup data-verseid=\"25\">&nbsp;<!-- -->25<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"25\">Ahih keileh puannel niknek a silh mi khat a en dinga pai na hi uh hiam? En un, puanhoih a silh minuamsate kumpi inn sungah a teengte ahi uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"26\"><sup data-verseid=\"26\">&nbsp;<!-- -->26<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"26\">Tua ahih leh bang en dinga pai na hi uh hiam? Kamsangpa khat a en dinga pai na hi uh hiam? Hi mah hi. Ken kong cih in ah, kamsang khat sangin a lianzawpa ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"27\"><sup data-verseid=\"27\">&nbsp;<!-- -->27<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"27\">Lai Siangtho ah a kigelh mah bangin, ‘En in, nangma lampi a sialkhol dingin, Na mai ah ka kamtaipa ka sawl hi,’ ci a, a kigelhpa in amah ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"28\"><sup data-verseid=\"28\">&nbsp;<!-- -->28<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"28\">“Banghang hiam cihleh ken kong cih in ah numei sung pana a suak mite lakah Tuiphumpa John sanga a lianzaw kamsang khat beek a om kei hi. -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"32\">Sumbuuk ah tu in, ‘Tamngai ka tumtum uh hangin, Na lam tuan kei uh a, Ka tam lawhlawh uh hangin, Na kap nuam kei uh hi,’ ci in khat le khat a kigal awtsan naupangte tawh na kibang uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"33\"><sup data-verseid=\"33\">&nbsp;<!-- -->33<!-- pai a, anne tuidawn in a om ciangin, ‘En un, anhaipa, zuhaipa, siahdongte le mimawhte lawmpa hi,’ na ci zel uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" khe kiangah amah dingin kap a, a khitui tawh Zeisu khe a kawtsak hi. A sam tawh a khe nulsak in nam a, sathau namtui tawh a zut hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"39\"><sup data-verseid=\"39\">&nbsp;<!-- -->39<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"39\">Zeisu a sam Pharisee pa in a muh ciangin, “Hihpa in kamsang taktak hi leh amah a lawng hih numei kua hi a, bangci bang mi hiam cih a thei ding hi.     "8": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">8</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Tua khit ciangin Zeisu in Pasian kumpigam tawh kipawl lungdamna thu a tangko ding le a hilh dingin khuapi khuaneu khempeuh ah zin kawikawi a, sawm le nihte in zong a zui uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Dawigilote bawlsiatna pan le natna panin damna a ngah numeite in zong a zui uh hi. Hih numeite in amaute neihsa tawh Zeisu a panpihte ahi uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Khua khempeuh pana hong pai mihonpite a hong kisuktuah khop uh ciangin Zeisu in thugentehna khat a gen inah,</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">“Khaici vawhpa khat khaici vawh dingin a kuankhia hi. Hih thu in, ‘Amaute in a etet uh hangin mu loin, A zakzak uh hangin a theih loh nading uh ahi hi.’</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">“Tu in thugentehna a khiatna in hih bang ahi hi. Tua laitak in tuilipi tungah huihpi hong nung a, gunkuang sungah tui dim dekdek ahih manin a lauhuai mahmah hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"24\"><sup data-verseid=\"24\">&nbsp;<!-- -->24<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"24\">Tua ciangin a nungzuite pai in amah phong uh a, “Sia aw, Sia aw, a simang khin ding ka hita uh hi!” a ci uh hi. Amah tho in huihpi le tuihual a taii ciangin tuate khawl in a dai pah dide hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"25\"><sup data-verseid=\"25\">&nbsp;<!-- -->25<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"25\">Tua ciangin amah in amaute kiangah, “Na upna uh koi ah om ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Amaute in lamdangsa in lau mahmah uh a, “Bangci bang mi ahi hiam? Thu a piak ciangin huihpi le tuihual nangawn in a thu a mang uh hi!” a kici uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"26\"><sup data-verseid=\"26\">&nbsp;<!-- -->26<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"26\">Tua ciangin Galilee tuilipi gal khat a om Gadara mite teenna kuam lamah gunkuang tuangin a galkah uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"27\"><sup data-verseid=\"27\">&nbsp;<!-- -->27<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"27\">Gunkuang tung pan Zeisu a kum khit phetin dawi a lutzawh a sawt khinzo tua khua mi khatin a na dawntuah hi. Nong bawlsiat loh nadingin kong thum hi!” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"29\"><sup data-verseid=\"29\">&nbsp;<!-- -->29<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"29\">Banghang hiam cihleh tua pa sung panin tua dawigilo a taikhiat nading Zeisu in thu a pia zo hi. Tua dawigilo in tua pa man pahpah ahih manin sikkhau tawh khih uh a, a khekol bulh in a cin uh hangin tua a kikhihnate peksat in dawi in gamlak ah a hawlkhia pahpah hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"30\"><sup data-verseid=\"30\">&nbsp;<!-- -->30<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"30\">Zeisu in, “Na min bang ahi hiam?” ci in a dot ciangin, amah in ama sungah dawi tampi om ahih manin, “Legionɠ,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"31\"><sup data-verseid=\"31\">&nbsp;<!-- -->31<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"31\">Tua dawite in mong neilo kuahawmpi sungah pai dingin thu a piak loh nadingin Zeisu kiangah a thum uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"32\"><sup data-verseid=\"32\">&nbsp;<!-- -->32<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"32\">Tua laitak in mual tungah vokhonpi khat gamta in a om hi. Dawite in tua vokte sungah amaute a lutsak nadingin Zeisu kiangah ngen uh a, Zeisu in a phal hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"33\"><sup data-verseid=\"33\">&nbsp;<!-- -->33<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"33\">Tua ciangin dawite zong tua pa sung panin paikhia in, vokte sungah a lut uh ciangin vokhonpite ken lakah taikeksuk uh a, tuili sung kidenna in a si khin uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"34\"><sup data-verseid=\"34\">&nbsp;<!-- -->34<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"34\">Vokcingte in tua thupiang teng a muh uh ciangin tai uh a, khuasung le gam sungteng ah a va gen uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"35\"><sup data-verseid=\"35\">&nbsp;<!-- -->35<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"35\">Tua ciangin thupiang teng en dingin khuasung mite hong pai uha Zeisu kianga tun uh ciangin dawite a taikhiatna pa in puansilh in lungsim ngeina pua in Zeisu khe phungah tu‑a a om a muh uh ciangin a lau uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"36\"><sup data-verseid=\"36\">&nbsp;<!-- -->36<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"36\">Dawite a lutna pa a damsak dan a mu mite in tua khua mite kiangah a gensawn uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"37\"><sup data-verseid=\"37\">&nbsp;<!-- -->37<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"37\">Tua ciangin Gadara kuam kima teeng mite khempeuh lau mahmah uh ahih manin amaute kiang pan Zeisu a paikhiat nadingin a ngen uh hi. Tua ciangin amah gunkuang tungah kah in a ciahkik hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"38\"><sup data-verseid=\"38\">&nbsp;<!-- -->38<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"38\">Tu in dawite a taikhiatna pa in Zeisu zui nuamin a kun hi. Ahih hangin Zeisu in ama kiangah,</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"39\"><sup data-verseid=\"39\">&nbsp;<!-- -->39<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"39\">“Na inn ah ciah inla, Pasian in nang aa dinga hong bawlsak nalianpite va gen in,” a ci hi. Tua pa ciahin Zeisu in ama aa dinga a bawl nalianpite khua sungteng ah a tangko hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"40\"><sup data-verseid=\"40\">&nbsp;<!-- -->40<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"40\">Mi khempeuh in Zeisu a tunkik ding ngaklah mahmah uh a, a tun ciangin a dawn uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"41\"><sup data-verseid=\"41\">&nbsp;<!-- -->41<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"41\">Tua laitak in Jairus kici kikhopna inn ukpa khat hong pai a, Zeisu khe phungah bokin a inn ah a hawh nadingin a thum hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"42\"><sup data-verseid=\"42\">&nbsp;<!-- -->42<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"42\">Banghang hiam cihleh kum sawm le kum nih a pha a tanu neihsun si dektak in a om hi. Zeisu a pai laitak in mihonpite in amah a phugawp uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"43\"><sup data-verseid=\"43\">&nbsp;<!-- -->43<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"43\">Tu in kum sawm le kum nih sung siluang natna a vei numei khat zong a om hi. Amah in a kivak nading teng nangawn siavuante guaihna in a zat khit hangin kuamah in a damsak zo kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"44\"><sup data-verseid=\"44\">&nbsp;<!-- -->44<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"44\">Tua nu in Zeisu nunglam panin zuana a puanmongtep a va lawn ciangin a siluang lai thakhat in a kang hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"45\"><sup data-verseid=\"45\">&nbsp;<!-- -->45<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"45\">Zeisu in, “Kua in hong lawng ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Mi khempeuh in a nial uh ciangin Peter le a lawmte in, “Sia aw, mihonpi hi zah ta in hong suknawk hong tonawk kimlai banghang in, ‘Kua in hong lawng hiam?’ cimawk na hi hiam?” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"46\"><sup data-verseid=\"46\">&nbsp;<!-- -->46<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"46\">Ahih hangin Zeisu in, “Mi khatin hong lawng mah hi. Banghang hiam cihleh ka sung pan vangliatna a paikhiat lam ka thei hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"47\"><sup data-verseid=\"47\">&nbsp;<!-- -->47<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"47\">Tua nu in kisel zolo ding ahihlam a theih ciangin lingkawmsa in Zeisu mai ah va bok a, amah a lawnna a hang le a lawn cianga a dam pahna thu mi khempeuh mai ah a gen hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"48\"><sup data-verseid=\"48\">&nbsp;<!-- -->48<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"48\">Tua ciangin Zeisu in ama kiangah, “Ka tanu aw, lungnuam in. Um peuh leteh amah a hingkik ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"51\"><sup data-verseid=\"51\">&nbsp;<!-- -->51<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"51\">Kikhopna inn ukpa inn ah Zeisu a tun ciangin Peter, James, John, le numeino nu le pate bek inn sungah a lutsak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"52\"><sup data-verseid=\"52\">&nbsp;<!-- -->52<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"52\">Tu in mi khempeuh in numeino nu sihna hangin kap le mau in a om ngeingai uh hi. Tua ciangin nek theih khatpeuh a piak nadingun thu a pia hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"56\"><sup data-verseid=\"56\">&nbsp;<!-- -->56<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"56\">A nu le a pa in lamdangsa mahmah uh a, ahi zongin Zeisu in kuama kiangah a gen loh nadingun thu a pia hi.</span></span></div><section class=\"information\"><button class=\"information-toggle\" type=\"button\">Copyrighted Material<!-- -->&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class=\"learn-more\">Learn More</span><svg class=\"icon\"><use xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" xlink:href=\"/svglist.svg#arrow_down\"></use></svg></button><div aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"rah-static rah-static--height-zero \" style=\"height:0;overflow:hidden\"><div><div style=\"max-height:0\" class=\"copyrights-section\"><div class=\"ot-copyright\"></div><div class=\"nt-copyright\"></div></div></div></div><div class=\"ministry-statement\"><div class=\"ministry-tagline\">©<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"http://www.bible.is\">Bible.is</a>, a ministry of<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.faithcomesbyhearing.com\">Faith Comes By Hearing</a>&nbsp;<!-- -->®.<!-- -->&nbsp;</div><div class=\"ministry-terms-support\"><a id=\"terms-of-service\" href=\"/terms\">Terms and Conditions</a>&nbsp; | &nbsp;<a href=\"https://support.bible.is/contact\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" id=\"help-support\">Help &amp; Support</a></div></div></section></main>",
    "9": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">9</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Tua khit ciangin Zeisu in a nungzui sawm le nihte khawm a, dawi khempeuh hawlkhiat theih nading le natna damsak theih nading vangliatna le thuneihna a piak khitteh,</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Pasian kumpigam thu a hilh ding le cinate a damsak dingin amaute a sawlkhia hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Amaute kiangah, “Lampi a na zat ding uh ciangkhut, thungip, nek theih le sum le pai a kipan bangmah keng kei un. Puanak silh nih kengthuah kei un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Na zin tunna peuhpeuh uhah tua khuapan na paikhiat masiah uh tamsuak un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Zin hong tungsaklo mi a om leh tua khuapan na paikhiat uh ciangin note khepek tunga leivuite singkhia un. Ama thu na mang un,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"36\"><sup data-verseid=\"36\">&nbsp;<!-- -->36<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"36\">Tua awging a khawl ciangin Zeisu bek a mu uh hi. Kei hong sang mi in kei hong sawlpa zong a sang ahi hi. Banghang hiam cihleh note khempeuh laka a neupenpa in a lianpenpa a suak ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"49\"><sup data-verseid=\"49\">&nbsp;<!-- -->49<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"49\">Tua ciangin John in, “Sia aw, nangma min tawh dawite a hawlkhia mi khat ka mu uh a, amah in eite hong zui lo ahih manin ka kham uh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"50\"><sup data-verseid=\"50\">&nbsp;<!-- -->50<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"50\">Zeisu in, “Kham kei un.     "10": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">10</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Hih thuteng khit ciangin Topa in a dang mi 70 sehkhia in a sawtlo a ama zin nading khuapi khuaneu khempeuh ah nihta nihta in a paikholsak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Amah in amaute kiangah, “An lak ding tam mahmah a, ahih hangin nasem ding mi a tawm hi. Tua ahih manin an nei Topa in ama an la dingin nasemte hong sawl nading thungen un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Note va kuankhia un. En un, ngiate laka kikhah tuunote bangin note kong khah hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Sumbawm, thungip, khedapte keng kei un. Lampi ah na pai laitak un kuamah hopih kei un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">“Inn khatpeuh ah na lut uh ciangin, ‘Hih inn ah nopna om tahen,’ ci masa un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Tua inn ah nopna ngah dinga kilawm mi a om leh note piak nopna tua inn ah tung dinga, a om kei leh note kiangah hong kilehkik ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">Inn khatah omsuak unla, zintunna khel kawikawi kei un. Ahi zongin Pasian kumpigam note kiang hong tung dekta hi cih theita un,’ ci in gen un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Ken kong cih in ah tua Ni ciangin tua khua in Sodom khuapi sangin gimna a thuak zaw ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">“Chorazin khua aw, gimna na thuak ding hi! Tua khit ciangin ama laa tungah pua in zintun buuk khatah paipih a, tualai ah a khoi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"35\"><sup data-verseid=\"35\">&nbsp;<!-- -->35<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"35\">A zingciang in sumtang denariusɠ nih lakhia in zintun buuk neipa pia a, ‘Hihpa na khoisak in. Hihteng bana na zat khempeuh kong paikik ciangin kong loh ding hi,’ ci in a paikhia hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"36\"><sup data-verseid=\"36\">&nbsp;<!-- -->36<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"36\">“Tua mi thumte sung panin kua pen a kisuam mipa vengpa hi dingin na ngaihsun hiam?” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"37\"><sup data-verseid=\"37\">&nbsp;<!-- -->37<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"37\">Thukhamhilh siapa in, “Amah a hehpihpa ahi hi,” a ci hi. Zeisu in ama kiangah, “Pai inla, nang zong tua bangin hih in,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"38\"><sup data-verseid=\"38\">&nbsp;<!-- -->38<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"38\">Zeisu le a nungzuite a pai kawmkawm un khua khatah amah lut a, Martha kici numei khatin a inn ah Zeisu a tungsak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"39\"><sup data-verseid=\"39\">&nbsp;<!-- -->39<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"39\">Martha in Mary kici sanggam numei khat nei a, tua nu Zeisu khephung ah tu in a thugente a ngai hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"40\"><sup data-verseid=\"40\">&nbsp;<!-- -->40<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"40\">Martha pen annek bawl in manlah ahih manin, Zeisu kiangah va pai a, “Topa aw, ka sanggamnu in annek bawl ding kei bek hong khiat awi na hi hiam? Hong huh nadingin sawl dih in,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"41\"><sup data-verseid=\"41\">&nbsp;<!-- -->41<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"41\">Zeisu in Martha kiangah, “Martha, Martha aw, lung hih mawhna na hau a, na lung a gim hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"42\"><sup data-verseid=\"42\">&nbsp;<!-- -->42<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"42\">Ahi zongin a kisam na khat bek om a, Mary in a hoih zaw tua na teel khin ahih manin a kilakkhiatsak kei ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span></div><section class=\"information\"><button class=\"information-toggle\" type=\"button\">Copyrighted Material<!-- -->&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class=\"learn-more\">Learn More</span><svg class=\"icon\"><use xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" xlink:href=\"/svglist.svg#arrow_down\"></use></svg></button><div aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"rah-static rah-static--height-zero \" style=\"height:0;overflow:hidden\"><div><div style=\"max-height:0\" class=\"copyrights-section\"><div class=\"ot-copyright\"></div><div class=\"nt-copyright\"></div></div></div></div><div class=\"ministry-statement\"><div class=\"ministry-tagline\">©<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"http://www.bible.is\">Bible.is</a>, a ministry of<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.faithcomesbyhearing.com\">Faith Comes By Hearing</a>&nbsp;<!-- -->®.<!-- -->&nbsp;</div><div class=\"ministry-terms-support\"><a id=\"terms-of-service\" href=\"/terms\">Terms and Conditions</a>&nbsp; | &nbsp;<a href=\"https://support.bible.is/contact\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" id=\"help-support\">Help &amp; Support</a></div></div></section></main>",
    "11": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">11</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Khatvei munkhat ah Zeisu in thungen a, a thunget a man ciangin a nungzuite khat in, “Topa aw, John in a nungzuite a hilh bangin ko zong thungetzia hong hilh in,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Tua ciangin amah in amaute kiangah, “Thu na nget uh ciangin hih bangin ngen un. Vantung a om kote Pa aw, Na min siangtho kizahtak hen. Na kumpigam hong tung tahen. Vantung ah na deihna a kisep mah bangin, Leitung ah zong kisem tahen.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Nisim a ka khamkhop ding uh, An hong pia in.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Ko tung a hong mawhte, Ka maisak mah bangun, Kote mawhna zong hong maisak ta in. Ze‑etna sungah hong lutsak kei in, Gilopa vangliatna pan hong honkhia in, ci in na ngen un,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Tua khit ciangin amah in, “Note lakah mi khatin lawmkhat nei in tua a lawmpa kiangah zankimpi in va pai in, ‘Lawm aw, anlum thum hong leitawisak in.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Ka lawmpa khat khualzin hong tung a, amah ka lui ding bangmah ka nei kei hi,’ a va ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">“Tua ciangin a lawmpa in a innsung panin, ‘Hong nawngkaisak kei in. Zong un, na mu ding uh hi. Kongkhak kiu un, hong kihon ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"10\"><sup data-verseid=\"10\">&nbsp;<!-- -->10<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"10\">Banghang hiam cihleh a ngen khempeuh in a ngah hi. A zong mi in a mu hi. Kong a kiu mi a kihon hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- Hi hi, ken kong cih in ah tua sisante tulai khang mite tungah a kisik ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"52\"><sup data-verseid=\"52\">&nbsp;<!-- -->52<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"52\">“Thukhamhilh siate aw, gimna na thuak ding uh hi! Banghang hiam cihleh thu theihna kong tawhtang nei napi in na kemcip uh hi. Note lah lut loin a lut nuam mite lah na khaktan uh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"53\"><sup data-verseid=\"53\">&nbsp;<!-- -->53<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"53\">Amah in hih thute a gen khit ciangin thukhamhilh siate le Pharisee pawlte in nakpitak in amah langpan uh a, thu tampi a leh lamlam in a dong huan uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"54\"><sup data-verseid=\"54\">&nbsp;<!-- -->54<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"54\">Ama kampauna tawh man a, a mawhmat theih nadingun a pangsim gige uh hi.</span></span></div><section class=\"information\"><button class=\"information-toggle\" type=\"button\">Copyrighted Material<!-- -->&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class=\"learn-more\">Learn More</span><svg class=\"icon\"><use xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" xlink:href=\"/svglist.svg#arrow_down\"></use></svg></button><div aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"rah-static rah-static--height-zero \" style=\"height:0;overflow:hidden\"><div><div style=\"max-height:0\" class=\"copyrights-section\"><div class=\"ot-copyright\"></div><div class=\"nt-copyright\"></div></div></div></div><div class=\"ministry-statement\"><div class=\"ministry-tagline\">©<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"http://www.bible.is\">Bible.is</a>, a ministry of<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.faithcomesbyhearing.com\">Faith Comes By Hearing</a>&nbsp;<!-- -->®.<!-- -->&nbsp;</div><div class=\"ministry-terms-support\"><a id=\"terms-of-service\" href=\"/terms\">Terms and Conditions</a>&nbsp; | &nbsp;<a href=\"https://support.bible.is/contact\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" id=\"help-support\">Help &amp; Support</a></div></div></section></main>",
    "12": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">12</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Tua laitak in sim zawhloh dinga a tam mihonpite hong kikaikhawm uh a, khat le khat kisik kha zah dongin om ngeingai uh hi. Zeisu in a nungzuite thu hilh masa a, “Pharisee pawlte kineihkhemna silngo na kidawm un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Banghang hiam cihleh a kilang lo dingin a kisincip, a kithei lo dinga kiselsim thei bangmah a om kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Tua ahih manin khuamial sunga na genteng uh khuavak sungah a kiza ding hi. Innsung tawnga na kigensim thute uh innkhumzang ah a kitangko khia ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">“Lawmte aw, ken kong gen in ah pumpi a thah theih hangin a dang bangmah a cih thei nawnlote kihta kei un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Ahi zongin na kihtak ding uh kua ahi hiam cih kong gen ding hi. Pumpi a thah khit ciangin hellɠ sungah khiat theihna thu a neipa na kihta un. Hi hi, ken kong cih in ah na kihtak ding uh tua pa ahi hi!</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Kawlgit nga ciangin dangkasanɠ nih tawh kizuak hilo ahi hiam? Pasian in tua kawlgitte khat nangawn a mangngilh kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">Note luzang a samzang omteng a vekpi in a kisim khinzo hi. Tua ahih manin lau kei un. Kawlgit tampi sangin na manpha zaw uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"8\"><sup data-verseid=\"8\">&nbsp;<!-- -->8<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"8\">“Ken kong cih in ah mite mai‑a kei hong pulak mi peuhmah Mihing Tapa in zong Pasian vantungmite mai ah a pulak ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"9\"><sup data-verseid=\"9\">&nbsp;<!-- -->9<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"9\">Mite mai‑a kei a hong nial peuhmah Pasian vantungmite mai ah ka nial ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"10\"><sup data-verseid=\"10\">&nbsp;<!-- -->10<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"10\">Tua hi a, Mihing Tapa langpan in a gensiate peuhmah a kimaisak ding hi. Ahi zongin Kha Siangtho tunga a pausia mi peuhmah a kimaisak kei ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">“Tu in kikhopna innte ah ahi a, makaite le thuneite mai ah ahi zongin note a hong paipih uh ciangin bang thu genin bangci gen ding ka hi uh hiam cih lungkham kei un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Banghang hiam cihleh tua hun ciangin Kha Siangtho in na gen ding uh thu a hong hilh ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">Tua laitak in mihonpi lak pan khatin, “Sia aw, ka sanggampa in ama gamh hong hop nading hong gensak in,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Ahih hangin Zeisu in ama kiangah, “Mipa aw, note tunga thukhen ding le note gamh hawm dingin kua in kei hong seh ahi hiam?” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">Tua ciangin amah in amaute kiangah, “Deihgawhna lungsim na neih khakloh nadingun hoihtak in kidawm un. Banghang hiam cihleh mihing nuntakna in neih le lam a bucin manin a kicing ahi kei hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"16\"><sup data-verseid=\"16\">&nbsp;<!-- -->16<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"16\">Tua khit ciangin amah in thugentehna khat gen a, “Mihaupa khat lo panin an tampi a piang hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"17\"><sup data-verseid=\"17\">&nbsp;<!-- -->17<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"17\">Tua ciangin amah in, ‘Ka an khol nading om nawnlo ahih manin bang cih leng hoih ding hiam?’ ci in a ngaihsun hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"18\"><sup data-verseid=\"18\">&nbsp;<!-- -->18<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"18\">“Tua ciangin amah in, ‘Hih bangin ka hih ding hi. Ka ansalte phelkhia in a lianzaw in ka lam dinga, ka an khempeuh le ka vanteng ka koih ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"19\"><sup data-verseid=\"19\">&nbsp;<!-- -->19<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"19\">Tua ciangin ka kha kiangah, “Ka kha aw, kum tampi na khom dingin na tampi kong kholsak zo hi. Om hithiat inla, nene dawndawn in, a nuam theithei in om in,” ka ci ding hi, ’ a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"20\"><sup data-verseid=\"20\">&nbsp;<!-- -->20<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"20\">“Ahih hangin Pasian in ama kiangah, ‘Mi haipa aw! Tuzan ciangin na kha kila ding hi. Na kholsa tua nate kua in ngah ding ahi hiam?’ a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"21\"><sup data-verseid=\"21\">&nbsp;<!-- -->21<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"21\">“Tua ahih manin ama aa ding bekin neihsa khol a, Pasian mai ah a khollo mi in tua pa tawh a kibang ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"22\"><sup data-verseid=\"22\">&nbsp;<!-- -->22<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"22\">Tua khit ciangin amah in a nungzuite kiangah, “Tua hi a, note kianga kong gen in ah bang ka ne ding hiam, ci in nuntak nading lungkham kei un. Bang silh dinga bang teeng ding ka hi hiam, ci in pumpi aa dingin lungkham kei un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"23\"><sup data-verseid=\"23\">&nbsp;<!-- -->23<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"23\">Nek le dawn sangin nuntakna thupi zaw a, silh le teen sangin pumpi a thupi zaw hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"24\"><sup data-verseid=\"24\">&nbsp;<!-- -->24<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"24\">Va‑aakte na lungngai un. Amaute in khaici tuh lo, an zong la loin, bem le sal zong a nei kei uh hi. Ahi zongin, Pasian in amaute an a vak hi. Vasate sangin note manpha zawtham hilo na hi uh hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"25\"><sup data-verseid=\"25\">&nbsp;<!-- -->25<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"25\">Na lungkham manun na tun sanna uh tong khat nangawn a khan thei kua om na hi uh hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"26\"><sup data-verseid=\"26\">&nbsp;<!-- -->26<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"26\">Hih bang thu neupen khat nangawn hih theilo na hih uh leh banghang in a dangte lungkham pih na hi uh hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"27\"><sup data-verseid=\"27\">&nbsp;<!-- -->27<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"27\">“Unok pakte khanzia ngaihsun dih un. Amaute in na sem loim khau zong a khek kei uh hi. Ahi zongin ken kong cih in ah Solomon in a minthanna puan tawh kizem a a om laitak nangawn in hih pakte khat zahin hoih zolo hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"28\"><sup data-verseid=\"28\">&nbsp;<!-- -->28<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"28\">Upna neu mite aw, tuni in lo lai ah po in, zingciang in mei‑a a kikhultum ding lopate nangawn Pasian in tua bangin zem ahih leh note hong zem zawkan lo ding ahi hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"29\"><sup data-verseid=\"29\">&nbsp;<!-- -->29<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"29\">Tua ahih manin na nek na dawn ding uh zong masa kei unla, lunghimawh kei un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"30\"><sup data-verseid=\"30\">&nbsp;<!-- -->30<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"30\">Banghang hiam cihleh leitung mite in tua nate zon masak in a nei uh hi. Hih nate na kisap lam uh na Pa un a hong thei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"31\"><sup data-verseid=\"31\">&nbsp;<!-- -->31<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"31\">Pasian kumpigam zong masa le uh teh hih nate a hong piakthuah ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"32\"><sup data-verseid=\"32\">&nbsp;<!-- -->32<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"32\">“Tuuhonte aw, lau kei un. Banghang hiam cihleh na Pa un note tungah kumpigam a hong piak ding pen ama lungkimna ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"33\"><sup data-verseid=\"33\">&nbsp;<!-- -->33<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"33\">Na neihsate uh zuak unla mizawngte huhna in zang un. Tua bangin a luitheilo sumbawm bawl unla a bei theilo dingin vantung ah sum na khol un. Tualai ah gutate in gu theilo in ngetin zong a ne thei kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"34\"><sup data-verseid=\"34\">&nbsp;<!-- -->34<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"34\">Banghang hiam cihleh na sum omna munah na lungsim zong a om ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"35\"><sup data-verseid=\"35\">&nbsp;<!-- -->35<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"35\">“Na kawng uh gak unla, na meivak uh vaksa in koih un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"36\"><sup data-verseid=\"36\">&nbsp;<!-- -->36<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"36\">A topa uh mopawi panin a hong ciahkik a hong tun ciangin, kong hong kiu dinga a hon thei pah dingin a ngak mite bangin na om un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"37\"><sup data-verseid=\"37\">&nbsp;<!-- -->37<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"37\">A topa uh hong ciah ciangin a na ngaka om a muh nasemte in mihampha ahi uh hi. Aman takpi kong cih in ah, amah in a kawnggak in a nasemte an ne dingin a tusak hi. Tua ciangin amah hong pai in an a lui hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"38\"><sup data-verseid=\"38\">&nbsp;<!-- -->38<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"38\">Amah zanvil nihna hunin hong tung ta leh, zanvil thumna hunin hong tung ta leh tua banga a om a muh nasemte in mihampha ahi uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"39\"><sup data-verseid=\"39\">&nbsp;<!-- -->39<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"39\">Ahi zongin hih thu thei un. Inn neipa in gutapa pai ding hun theikhol hi leh pang gige in a inn a luhsak kei ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"40\"><sup data-verseid=\"40\">&nbsp;<!-- -->40<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"40\">Tua ahih ciangin na upmawh loh laitak un Mihing Tapa hong pai ding ahih manin note zong kigingsa in om un,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"41\"><sup data-verseid=\"41\">&nbsp;<!-- -->41<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"41\">Tua ciangin Peter in ama kiangah, “Topa aw, hih thugentehna kote aa ding beka nong gen ahi hiam? Ahih keileh mi khempeuh aa dinga na gen ahi hiam?” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"42\"><sup data-verseid=\"42\">&nbsp;<!-- -->42<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"42\">Tua ciangin Topa in, “A hun a tun ciangin a innkuanpihte annek tuidawn ding a vaihawmsak dinga a topa in a koih, a muanhuai le a lungpil neihsa kempa kua ahi hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"43\"><sup data-verseid=\"43\">&nbsp;<!-- -->43<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"43\">A topa hong tun ciangin tua banga om nasem a muh nasempa in mihampha ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"44\"><sup data-verseid=\"44\">&nbsp;<!-- -->44<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"44\">Aman takpi kong cih in ah, amah in a neihsa khempeuh tua nasempa a uksak ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"45\"><sup data-verseid=\"45\">&nbsp;<!-- -->45<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"45\">Ahih hangin tua nasempa in a lungsim sungah, ‘Ka topa hong tungbaih nailo ding hi,’ ci in, a topa nasemte, numei pasal ci loin satin vua henla, anne tuidawn, zukham ankham in om leh,</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"46\"><sup data-verseid=\"46\">&nbsp;<!-- -->46<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"46\">a lametloh ni le a theihloh kalin a topa hong tungvat dinga, a topa in tua nasempa tumnih suahin thu‑umlote tawh a thuakkhawmsak ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"47\"><sup data-verseid=\"47\">&nbsp;<!-- -->47<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"47\">“A topa deihna thei napi in kiging lo a, a topa deihna banga a semlo nasempa in tamveipi satna a thuak ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"48\"><sup data-verseid=\"48\">&nbsp;<!-- -->48<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"48\">Ahi zongin a topa deihna a theih loh manin a sathuai nasep a sem kha nasempa in a tawm zaw satna a thuak ding hi. Banghang hiam cihleh tampi a kipia mi tung panin a tam zaw kisikkik dinga, tampi a ki‑apte tung panin a tam zaw a kingenkik ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"49\"><sup data-verseid=\"49\">&nbsp;<!-- -->49<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"49\">“Leitung ah meikuang khah dinga hong pai ka hi a, tua mei a kuang khin hi leh ka ut hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"50\"><sup data-verseid=\"50\">&nbsp;<!-- -->50<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"50\">Ahi zongin ka thuak ding baptize na khat om a, tua ka zawh mateng ka lung a gim mahmah hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"51\"><sup data-verseid=\"51\">&nbsp;<!-- -->51<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"51\">Leitung ah kilemna piangsak dinga hong pai hong sa na hi uh hiam? Hi peuhmah lo hi. Kikhenna a piangsak dinga hong pai ka hi zaw hi cih thu kong gen hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"52\"><sup data-verseid=\"52\">&nbsp;<!-- -->52<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"52\">Banghang hiam cihleh tu a kipan inn khat sungah mi nga a om leh kilangkhenna om dinga, thumte in nih langah nihte in thum langah a pang ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"53\"><sup data-verseid=\"53\">&nbsp;<!-- -->53<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"53\">“A pa in a tapa langpan dinga, a ta in a pa a langpan ding hi. A nu in a tanu langpan dinga, a tanu in a nu a langpan ding hi. A teknu in a monu langpan dinga, a monu in a teknu a langpan ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"54\"><sup data-verseid=\"54\">&nbsp;<!-- -->54<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"54\">Tua khit ciangin amah in mihonpite kiangah, “Nitumna lam pan meii hong kai ciangin, ‘Guahzu ding hi,’ na ci uh a, guah hong zu takpi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"55\"><sup data-verseid=\"55\">&nbsp;<!-- -->55<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"55\">Leitaw lam pan huih hong nun ciangin, ‘Khualum ding hi,’ na ci uh a, khua a hong lum takpi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"56\"><sup data-verseid=\"56\">&nbsp;<!-- -->56<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"56\">A kineihkhem mite aw, van le lei omzia khentel thei napi uh cin banghang in tuhun omzia khentel theilo na hi uh hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"57\"><sup data-verseid=\"57\">&nbsp;<!-- -->57<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"57\">“Hi hi, banghang in no le no in thu a maan bangin khen theilo na hi uh hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"58\"><sup data-verseid=\"58\">&nbsp;<!-- -->58<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"58\">Na langpa tawh thukhen zum zuana na pai laitak in amah tawh na kilemkik theihtheih nadingin lamkal ah na hih theihtawp in hanciam in. Tua banga na hih kei leh amah in thukhenpa mai ah hong tun dinga, thukhenpa in palik bupa tungah hong piakhia in palik bupa in thongah hong khum ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"59\"><sup data-verseid=\"59\">&nbsp;<!-- -->59<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"59\">Ken kong cih in ah na liausum dangka na piak khit mateng in thong pan na suakta kei ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span></div><section class=\"information\"><button class=\"information-toggle\" type=\"button\">Copyrighted Material<!-- -->&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class=\"learn-more\">Learn More</span><svg class=\"icon\"><use xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" xlink:href=\"/svglist.svg#arrow_down\"></use></svg></button><div aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"rah-static rah-static--height-zero \" style=\"height:0;overflow:hidden\"><div><div style=\"max-height:0\" class=\"copyrights-section\"><div class=\"ot-copyright\"></div><div class=\"nt-copyright\"></div></div></div></div><div class=\"ministry-statement\"><div class=\"ministry-tagline\">©<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"http://www.bible.is\">Bible.is</a>, a ministry of<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.faithcomesbyhearing.com\">Faith Comes By Hearing</a>&nbsp;<!-- -->®.<!-- -->&nbsp;</div><div class=\"ministry-terms-support\"><a id=\"terms-of-service\" href=\"/terms\">Terms and Conditions</a>&nbsp; | &nbsp;<a href=\"https://support.bible.is/contact\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" id=\"help-support\">Help &amp; Support</a></div></div></section></main>",
    "13": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">13</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Tua laitak in Zeisu tawh a omkhawm mi pawlkhat in, Galilee mi pawlkhatte sisan le amaute biakna gan sisante Pilate in a helna thu ama kiangah a ko uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Tua ciangin Zeisu in amaute kiangah, “Hih Galilee mite in tua banga a thuak manun a dang Galilee mi khempeuh sangin a mawh zaw uh hi, ci in ngaihsun na hi uh hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">A mawh zaw kei uh hi, ci in kong gen hi.     "14": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">14</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Sabbath ni khatin Pharisee pawlte laka makai khatpa inn ah an ne dingin Zeisu pai a, amaute in Zeisu a encik uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">En in, cibawk natna a nei pasal khat ama mai ah a om hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Zeisu in thukhamhilh siate le Pharisee pawlte kiangah, “Sabbath ni‑a cina damsak ding thukham tawh a kituak hiam?” ci in a dong hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Ahih hangin amaute pau loin a om uh hi. Tua ciangin amah in cinapa samin damsak a, a ciahsak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Tua khit ciangin amaute kiangah, “Na laa khat uh, ahih keileh na bawng khat uh Sabbath ni in guam sungah kia leh a lakhia pah lo ding kua om na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Amaute in hih thute a dawngkik thei kei uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">Zeisu in an ne dinga a kisam mi pawlkhatte in munhoih tata a teel uh a muh ciangin, amaute kiangah thugentehna khat gen a,</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"8\"><sup data-verseid=\"8\">&nbsp;<!-- -->8<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"8\">“Mi khatin mopawi ah a hong kisap ciangin mun hoihpen ah tu kei un. Nang sanga a zahtakhuai zaw mi khat na kisam henla,</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"9\"><sup data-verseid=\"9\">&nbsp;<!-- -->9<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"9\">a sampa le tua pa hong pai in, ‘Na tutna hihpa na awn in,’ hong ci leh maizum in a niampen munah na tu ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"10\"><sup data-verseid=\"10\">&nbsp;<!-- -->10<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"10\">Mopawi ah a hong kisap ciangin a niampen munah tu leteh hong sampa hong pai ciangin, ‘Lawm aw, a sangah tuto in,’ hong ci dinga, na ankuang umpihte mai ah na mai tang ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">Banghang hiam cihleh amah le amah a kilamsang mi peuhmah kiniamkhiat dinga, amah le amah a kiniamkhiat mi kilamsang ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Tua khit ciangin Zeisu in a sampa kiangah zong, “Sun an ne ding ahi zongin nitak an ne ding ahi zongin mi na sap ciangin na lawmte, na sanggamte, na tanaute, na innveng mihaute khawng sam kei in. Tua mite sam leteh amaute in zong nang hong samkik in hong thukkik ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">Ahi zongin pawi na bawl ciangin mizawng, mipoi, khebai le mittawte sam in.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Amaute in hong thukkik zolo ding uh ahih manin thupha na ngah dinga, midikte thawhkik ni ciangin Pasian in a hong thukkik ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">Tu in amah tawh ankuang a umkhawm mi khatin hih thu a zak ciangin ama kiangah, “Pasian kumpigam sunga an a ne kha ding mi in mihampha ahi hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"16\"><sup data-verseid=\"16\">&nbsp;<!-- -->16<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"16\">Tua ciangin Zeisu in ama kiangah, “Mi khatin pawi lianpi khat bawla mitampi a sam hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"17\"><sup data-verseid=\"17\">&nbsp;<!-- -->17<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"17\">Annek hun ciangin a khohsa mite kiangah a nasempa sawl a, ‘Na khempeuh a baihsa in om hi. Hong paita un,’ ci in a gensak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"18\"><sup data-verseid=\"18\">&nbsp;<!-- -->18<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"18\">“Ahih hangin amaute khempeuh in paulap zong ciat uh a, a masapenpa in, ‘Lo khat lei khin ka hih manin pai in ka va et kul ding hi, hong theisiam in,’ a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"19\"><sup data-verseid=\"19\">&nbsp;<!-- -->19<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"19\">“A dang khatpa in, ‘Bawngtal kap nga ka lei khin a, ka va sin kul ding hi hong theisiam in,’ a ci leuleu hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"20\"><sup data-verseid=\"20\">&nbsp;<!-- -->20<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"20\">“A dang khatpa in zong, ‘Zi nei khin phet ka hih manin kong paithei kei ding hi,’ a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"21\"><sup data-verseid=\"21\">&nbsp;<!-- -->21<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"21\">“Tua ciangin tua nasempa hong ciahkik in a topa kiangah tua thuteng a gen hi.
