    "16": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">16</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Tua banah, Zeisu in a nungzuite kiangah, “Mihau khatin neihsa kempa khat a nei hi. Tua neihsa kempa in a topa neihsate thangzatgawp hi ci in a topa tungah a kikhia hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Tua ciangin amah in a neihsa kempa sam a, ‘Na thu ka zakte bangci bang ahi hiam? Ka neihsa kempa hi thei nawnlo ding na hih manin na sum zatna sazian hong pia in,’ a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">“Tua ciangin neihsa kempa in, ‘Ka topa in neihsa kem za panin hong tawpsak ding hita ahih manin bang cih ding ka hiam? Lei tawh ding lah ka ngap kei a, khutdawh nget ding lah ka maizum hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Neihsa kem za pan ka zakiat ciangin mite in amau inn a hong tunsak nop nadingun ka hih dingzia ka thei hi,’ ci in a lungsim sungah a ngaihsun hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">“Tua ciangin a topa tunga leiba a nei khempeuhte sam a, a khatna pa kiangah, ‘Ka topa tungah bangzah ba na hi hiam?’ a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Tua pa in, ‘Sathau bung 100 ka ba hi,’ a ci hi. Tua ciangin amah in tua pa kiangah, ‘Na leiba ciaptehna lai la inla tu pakin 50 in gelh mengmeng in,’ a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">“Tua khit ciangin a dang khatpa kiangah, ‘Nang bangzah na ba hiam?’ a cih ciangin, ‘Mangbuh bem 100 ka ba hi,’ a ci hi. Amah in, ‘Na leiba ciaptehna lai la inla, 80 in gelh in,’ a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"8\"><sup data-verseid=\"8\">&nbsp;<!-- -->8<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"8\">“Tua hi a, a thumanlo neihsa kempa in, khelpilna tawh a sep manin a topa in a phat hi. Banghang hiam cihleh tulai khang mite in amaute khanpih khuavak tate sangin a khelpil zaw uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"9\"><sup data-verseid=\"9\">&nbsp;<!-- -->9<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"9\">“Ken kong cih in ah hih leitung sum le pai tawh lawm le gual na zong un. Tua hi leh bangmah na neih nawnloh uh ciangin amaute in a tawntung in nang hong sang ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"10\"><sup data-verseid=\"10\">&nbsp;<!-- -->10<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"10\">“Thuneupen tungah a muanhuai mi in thuliante tungah zong a muanhuai hi. Thuneupen tunga diktatlo mi in thuliante tungah zong a diktat kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">Tua ahih manin leitung sum le pai tungah muanhuai kei le uhteh, kua in sum taktak hong ap ngam ding ahi hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Midang khat neihsa tungah muanhuai kei le uh teh kua in a neihsa uh note hong pia ding ahi hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">“Nasem khatin to nih na semkhawm theilo hi. Pasian na le leitung na na semkhawm thei kei ding uh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Tu in sumduh Pharisee pawlte in hih thu khempeuh a zak uh ciangin amah zahpih in a nuihsan uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">Tua ciangin amah in amaute kiangah, “Mite mai ah no le no na kidiksak uh hangin Pasian in na lungsim uh a thei hi. A kimasa numei a teenpih mi zong angkawm ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"19\"><sup data-verseid=\"19\">&nbsp;<!-- -->19<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"19\">“Khatvei lai in mihaupa khat om a, amah in puan dupsan le puanpak silhin nisim in leitung nopsakna tawh a om hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"20\"><sup data-verseid=\"20\">&nbsp;<!-- -->20<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"20\">Ahi zongin a inn kongpi gei ah a pumtang in meima a vei Lazarus kici khutdawh ngenpa khat a kikoih hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"21\"><sup data-verseid=\"21\">&nbsp;<!-- -->21<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"21\">Amah in mihaupa ankuang pana anneng kiate duhgawh mahmah in a om laitak in uite hong pai in a meimate a liak uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"22\"><sup data-verseid=\"22\">&nbsp;<!-- -->22<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"22\">“Tua nung ciangin khutdawh ngenpa si a, vantungmite in amah Abraham ang sungah a tun uh hi.     "17": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">17</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Tua ciangin Zeisu in a nungzuite kiangah, “Pukna a hong tun loh a phamawh thu hi a, ahi zongin tua pukna a piangsakpa in gimna a thuak ding hi!</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Mi khatin hih naupangnote khat a puksak sangin a ngawngah angawina suangtum khat khai in tuipi sungah kikhia leh ama aa dingin hoih zaw ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Tua ahih ciangin kikepsiam un.     "18": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">18</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Tua khit ciangin lungkialo a thu a nget tawntung nadingun Zeisu in thugentehna khat tawh amaute thu hilh a,</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">“Khua khatah Pasian a kihta lo, mi zong a thusimlo thukhenpa khat a om hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Tu in tua khua mahah meigongnu khat zong a om hi. anlum la in lungdam ko a, balkham in, “Hih in note aa dinga kipia ka pumpi ahi hi.
